    	  $(this).find('ul').hide();
    	  $(this).find('.classify_bg').hide();
      })
   })     
</script>

    	<div class="title_help">公司介绍</div>
                <div class="help_con">
            <h4>配送范围和时间</h4>
                        <p style="line-height:115%"><span style="font-size:12px;line-height:115%;font-family:宋体"><br /></span></p><p style="line-height:115%"><span style="font-size:12px;line-height:115%;font-family:宋体">抠抠网所有商品均由入驻商家负责配送，配送产生的运费也由商家规定。</span></p><p style="line-height:115%"><span style="font-size:12px;line-height:115%;font-family:宋体"><br /></span></p><p style="line-height:115%"><span style="font-size:12px;line-height:115%;font-family:arial, sans-serif">1</span><span style="font-size:12px;line-height:115%;font-family:宋体">、免运费</span></p><p style="line-height:115%"><span style="font-size:12px;line-height:115%;font-family:宋体"><br /></span></p><p style="line-height:115%"><span style="font-size:12px;line-height:115%;font-family:宋体">商家设定配送范围内的收货地址均不收取运费。客户购买此类商品无需支付运费。</span></p><p style="line-height:115%"><span style="font-size:12px;line-height:115%;font-family:宋体"><br /></span></p><p style="line-height:115%"><span style="font-size:12px;line-height:115%;font-family:arial, sans-serif">2</span><span style="font-size:12px;line-height:115%;font-family:宋体">、满额免运费</span></p><p style="line-height:115%"><span style="font-size:12px;line-height:115%;font-family:宋体"><br /></span></p><p style="line-height:115%"><span style="font-size:12px;line-height:115%;font-family:宋体">商家设定在商家店铺内购物满一定金额即可享受免收运费的优惠政策。当客户在一个商家店铺内购买此商家商品达到一定金额后，</span><span style="font-size:12px;line-height:115%;font-family:宋体">无须支付运费。</span></p><p style="line-height:115%"><span style="font-size:12px;line-height:115%;font-family:宋体"><br /></span></p><p style="line-height:115%"><span style="font-size:12px;line-height:115%;font-family:arial, sans-serif">3</span><span style="font-size:12px;line-height:115%;font-family:宋体">、按地区收取</span></p><p style="line-height:115%"><span style="font-size:12px;line-height:115%;font-family:宋体"><br /></span></p><p style="line-height:115%"><span style="font-size:12px;line-height:115%;font-family:宋体">商家对发往不同地区，不同重量的包裹所需的运费进行设定。客户购买此类商品时，系统会根据商家设定自动计算所需运费。客户须连同商品及运费共同支</span></p><p style="line-height:115%"><span style="font-size:12px;line-height:115%;font-family:宋体"><br /></span></p><p style="line-height:115%"><span style="font-size:12px;line-height:115%;font-family:宋体">付。</span></p><p style="line-height:115%"><span style="font-size:12px;line-height:115%;font-family:宋体"><br /></span></p><p style="line-height:115%"><span style="font-size:12px;line-height:115%;font-family:arial, sans-serif">4</span><span style="font-size:12px;line-height:115%;font-family:宋体">、发货时效</span></p><p style="line-height:115%"><span style="font-size:12px;line-height:115%;font-family:宋体"><br /></span></p><p style="line-height:115%"><span style="font-size:12px;line-height:115%;font-family:宋体">普通商品一般在客户下单后</span><span style="font-size:12px;line-height:115%;font-family:arial, sans-serif">1-2</span><span style="font-size:12px;line-height:115%;font-family:宋体">天内发出，团购和促销商品一般在客户购买后</span><span style="font-size:12px;line-height:115%;font-family:arial, sans-serif">72</span><span style="font-size:12px;line-height:115%;font-family:宋体">小时内发出。</span></p><p style="line-height:115%"><span style="font-size:12px;line-height:115%;font-family:宋体"><br /></span></p><p style="line-height:115%"><span style="font-size:12px;line-height:115%;font-family:arial, sans-serif">5</span><span style="font-size:12px;line-height:115%;font-family:宋体">、快递方式</span></p><p style="line-height:115%"><span style="font-size:12px;line-height:115%;font-family:宋体"><br /></span></p><p style="line-height:115%"><span style="font-size:12px;line-height:115%;font-family:宋体">购买商家商品时，由商家指定快递公司为您配送，如您有特殊需求，可以联系商家协商发货快递。</span></p><p style="line-height:115%"><br /></p>                    </div>
            </div>
    <!--内容end-->
    
</div>
